Layer-2 VPN connections:

Legend for connection status (St)   
EI -- encapsulation invalid      NC -- interface encapsulation not CCC/TCC/VPLS
EM -- encapsulation mismatch     WE -- interface and instance encaps not same
VC-Dn -- Virtual circuit down    NP -- interface hardware not present 
CM -- control-word mismatch      -> -- only outbound connection is up
CN -- circuit not provisioned    <- -- only inbound connection is up
OR -- out of range               Up -- operational
OL -- no outgoing label          Dn -- down                      
LD -- local site signaled down   CF -- call admission control failure      
RD -- remote site signaled down  SC -- local and remote site ID collision
LN -- local site not designated  LM -- local site ID not minimum designated
RN -- remote site not designated RM -- remote site ID not minimum designated
XX -- unknown connection status  IL -- no incoming label
MM -- MTU mismatch               MI -- Mesh-Group ID not available
BK -- Backup connection	         ST -- Standby connection
PF -- Profile parse failure      PB -- Profile busy
RS -- remote site standby	 SN -- Static Neighbor
LB -- Local site not best-site   RB -- Remote site not best-site
VM -- VLAN ID mismatch           HS -- Hot-standby Connection

Legend for interface status 
Up -- operational           
Dn -- down

policy-options {
    policy-statement NVN_EXPORT_SOO {
        term NVN_EXPORT_SOO {
            from community NVN_RJCT_SOO;
        }
        term T1 {
            from community NVN_RJCT_SOO;
            then reject;
        }
    }
    policy-statement NVN_IMPORT_SOO {
        term T1 {
            then {
                community add NVN_ADD_SOO;
                accept;
            }
        }
    }
    policy-statement ebgp-emix-export {
        term local-public {
            from {
                protocol aggregate;
                route-filter 31.219.182.0/24 orlonger;
            }
            then accept;
        }
        term lo0-public {
            from {
                protocol direct;
                interface lo0.100;
                route-filter 31.219.179.0/24 prefix-length-range /32-/32;
            }
            then accept;
        }
        term reject {
            then reject;
        }
    }
    policy-statement ebgp-ipsec-export {
        term loopback {
            from {
                protocol direct;
                route-filter 4.0.0.0/8 prefix-length-range /32-/32;
            }
            then accept;
        }
    }
    policy-statement ecmp {
        term ecmp {
            then {
                load-balance per-packet;
            }
        }
    }
    policy-statement ibgp-nhself {
        term ibgp {
            then {
                next-hop self;
            }
        }
    }
    policy-statement l3vpn-grx-ibgp-export {
        term deny-loopbacks {
            from {
                route-filter 1.0.0.0/24 prefix-length-range /32-/32;
                route-filter 1.0.1.0/24 prefix-length-range /32-/32;
            }
            then reject;
        }
        term ebgp-nhself {
            from {
                protocol bgp;
                route-type external;
            }
            then {
                next-hop self;
            }
        }
    }
    policy-statement local-pref-200 {
        term 1 {
            from protocol bgp;
            then {
                local-preference 200;
            }
        }
    }
    policy-statement lsdist-to-bgp {
        term te {
            from family traffic-engineering;
            then accept;
        }
    }
    policy-statement ted-to-lsdist {
        term te {
            from family traffic-engineering;
            then accept;
        }
    }
    community NVN_ADD_SOO members [ origin:8966:1 origin:64517:13 ];
    community NVN_RJCT_SOO members [ origin:8966:2 origin:64517:13 ];
}

    interfaces {
        xe-0/1/0 {
            unit 500 {
                forwarding-class expedited-forwarding;
            }
            unit 600 {
                forwarding-class expedited-forwarding;
            }
        }
    }
}
firewall {
    family inet {
        filter clear-df-bit {
            interface-specific;
            term grx-external-connection {
                from {
                    fragment-flags dont-fragment;
                }
                then {
                    count df-set-bits;
                    dont-fragment clear;
                }
            }
            term accept-any {
                then accept;
            }
        }
        filter ipv4-sampling {
            term sample {
                then {
                    sample;
                    accept;
                }
            }
        }
    }
    family mpls {
        filter sample {
            term sample-all {
                then {
                    sample;
                    accept;
                }
            }
        }
    }
    policer 1Mbps {
        if-exceeding {
            bandwidth-limit 1m;
            burst-size-limit 1500;
        }
        then discard;
    }
}

                    neighbor 3.0.15.2 {
                        peer-as 15;
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }
}
</configuration-text>
